msg:The most unsatisfactory hotel on this trip. Except for the mattress, which is soft and hard enough, it has almost no advantages.

The bathroom setting is completely inhumane. There is no place to put the mobile phone. The mobile phone can only be placed on the back cover of the toilet. The cover is curved and will slide off if you are not careful. The worn and yellowed bath towels with split edges are disgusting.

The so-called hot spring on the roof should be the biggest gimmick. I hope it is a hot spring. It is completely unbearable when the weather is a little cold, and the water quality is also very turbid.

The most unimaginable thing is that in a hotel that costs 800 or 900 yuan a night, even the fried eggs for breakfast are hidden behind the counter. You can't see them if you don't ask. Even asking for two fried eggs is considered a luxury. Even the breakfast of a fast hotel that costs 300 or 400 yuan will not be so stingy. The artificially synthesized fake ham full of flavors and spices makes you feel sick after eating a piece.

The service is all perfunctory. When checking in, you are asked to fill out a form to choose a few drinks. If you don't ask, you won't be served in the end.

The boss really knows how to make a fortune.

A hotel that I will never come to again.
